diplomatic_decisions = {

	buy_resource_aluminium_from_GER = {

		potential = {
			exists = GER
			has_country_flag = aluminium_trades_active
			GER = {
				or = {
					and = {
						check_variable = { which = "aluminium_building_balance" value = 1001 }
						not = { check_variable = { which = "aluminium_building_balance" value = 1002 } }
						not = { check_variable = { which = "aluminium_trade_sell" value = 1 } }
					}
					and = {
						check_variable = { which = "aluminium_building_balance" value = 1002 }
						not = { check_variable = { which = "aluminium_building_balance" value = 1003 } }
						not = { check_variable = { which = "aluminium_trade_sell" value = 2 } }
					}
					and = {
						check_variable = { which = "aluminium_building_balance" value = 1003 }

					and = {

						not = { check_variable = { which = "aluminium_building_balance" value = 1011 } }
						not = { check_variable = { which = "aluminium_trade_sell" value = 10 } }
					}
					and = {
						check_variable = { which = "aluminium_building_balance" value = 1011 }
						not = { check_variable = { which = "aluminium_building_balance" value = 1012 } }
						not = { check_variable = { which = "aluminium_trade_sell" value = 11 } }
					}
					and = {
						check_variable = { which = "aluminium_building_balance" value = 1012 }
						not = { check_variable = { which = "aluminium_building_balance" value = 1013 } }
						not = { check_variable = { which = "aluminium_trade_sell" value = 12 } }

					and = {

					and = {

						not = { check_variable = { which = "aluminium_building_balance" value = 1015 } }
						not = { check_variable = { which = "aluminium_trade_sell" value = 14 } }
					}
					and = {
						check_variable = { which = "aluminium_building_balance" value = 1015 }
						not = { check_variable = { which = "aluminium_building_balance" value = 1016 } }
						not = { check_variable = { which = "aluminium_trade_sell" value = 15 } }
					}
					and = {
						check_variable = { which = "aluminium_building_balance" value = 1016 }
						not = { check_variable = { which = "aluminium_building_balance" value = 1017 } }
						not = { check_variable = { which = "aluminium_trade_sell" value = 16 } }
					}
					and = {
						check_variable = { which = "aluminium_building_balance" value = 1017 }
						not = { check_variable = { which = "aluminium_building_balance" value = 1018 } }
						not = { check_variable = { which = "aluminium_trade_sell" value = 17 } }
					}

						not = { check_variable = { which = "aluminium_building_balance" value = 1019 } }
						not = { check_variable = { which = "aluminium_trade_sell" value = 18 } }
					}
					and = {
						check_variable = { which = "aluminium_building_balance" value = 1019 }
						not = { check_variable = { which = "aluminium_building_balance" value = 1020 } }
						not = { check_variable = { which = "aluminium_trade_sell" value = 19 } }
					}
					and = {
						check_variable = { which = "aluminium_building_balance" value = 1020 }
						not = { check_variable = { which = "aluminium_building_balance" value = 1021 } }
						not = { check_variable = { which = "aluminium_trade_sell" value = 20 } }
					}
				}
			}
			not = { war_with = GER }
			not = { tag = GER }
		}

		allow = {
			money = 2000
		}
		effect = {
			GER = { country_event = 13302 }
			add_country_modifier = {
				name = "aluminium_trade_buy_cooldown"
				duration = 7
			}
		}

		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 1
		}
	}
